Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 210 (Apollo 15-17 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Jim Lawton, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 210 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY 
	BY NASA 2021112-161 17:11 MAR. 19,1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

022398,000031:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
022399,000032:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022400,000033:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022401,000034:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022402,000035:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022403,000036: 
022404,000037:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
022405,000038:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
022406,000039:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
022407,000040:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
022408,000041:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022409,000042: 
022410,000043:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
022411,000044:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022412,000045:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
022413,000046:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
022414,000047:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
022415,000048:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
022416,000049:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
022417,000050:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
022418,000051:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
022419,000052:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
022420,000053:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)    
022421,000054:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
022422,000055:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022423,000056:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022424,000057:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022425,000058:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022426,000059:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
022427,000060:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022428,000061:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
022429,000062:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022430,000063:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022431,000064:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
022432,000065:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022433,000066:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
022434,000067: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
022435,000068: 
022436,000069: 33,2113                                           BANK     33                                    
022437,000070: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
022438,000071: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
022439,000072: 
022440,000073: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022441,000074: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
022442,000075: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
022443,000076: 24,2000           05331        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022444,000077: 24,2001           00004                           OCT      4                                     
022445,000078: 24,2002           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022446,000079: 24,2003           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26

022922,000555:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022923,000556:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022924,000557:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022925,000558:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022926,000559:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022927,000560: 
022928,000561:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022929,000562:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022930,000563:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022931,000564:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022932,000565:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022933,000566:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022934,000567:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022935,000568:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022936,000569:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022937,000570:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022938,000571:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022939,000572:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022940,000573:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022941,000574:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022942,000575:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022943,000576:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022944,000577:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022945,000578:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022946,000579:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022947,000580:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022948,000581:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022949,000582:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022950,000583: 24,2462  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022951,000584: 24,2462                                           COUNT*   $$/P25                                
022952,000585: 24,2462           05331        PROG25             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022953,000586: 24,2463           00004                           OCT      4                                     #  MAKE GROUP 4 INACTIVE (VERB 37)
022954,000587: 24,2464           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022955,000588: 24,2465           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022956,000589: 
022957,000590: 24,2466           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022958,000591: 24,2467           33757                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
022959,000592: 24,2470           05506                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022960,000593: 24,2471           00031                           ADRES    TRACKFLG                              #  SET TRACK FLAG
022961,000594: 24,2472           05506                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022962,000595: 24,2473           00006                           ADRES    P25FLAG                               #  SET P25FLAG
022963,000596: 24,2474           05520                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              
022964,000597: 24,2475           00010                           ADRES    RNDVZFLG                              
022965,000598: 24,2476           05355        P25LEM1            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022966,000599: 24,2477           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022967,000600: 24,2500           34734                           CAF      P25FLBIT                              
022968,000601: 24,2501           70074                           MASK     STATE                                 #  IS P25FLAG SET
022969,000602: 24,2502           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022970,000603: 24,2503           15146                           BZF      ENDOFJOB                              
022971,000604: 24,2504           34740                           CAF      TRACKBIT                              #  IS TRACKFLAG SET?

Page 519 

022973,000606: 24,2505           70075                           MASK     STATE      +1                         
022974,000607: 24,2506           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022975,000608: 24,2507           12515                           BZF      P25LMWT1                              #  NO-SKIP PHASE CHANGE AND WAIT 1 MINUTE
022976,000609: 24,2510           34750                           CAF      SEVEN                                 #  CALL R65 - FINE PREFERRED
022977,000610: 24,2511           55745                           TS       R65CNTR                               
022978,000611: 24,2512           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              #  TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE

022994,000627:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
022995,000628:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022996,000629:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022997,000630:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022998,000631:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022999,000632: 
023000,000633:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
023001,000634:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
023002,000635:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023003,000636:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023004,000637:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
023005,000638:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
023006,000639:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
023007,000640:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
023008,000641:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
023009,000642:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023010,000643:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
023011,000644:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
023012,000645:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
023013,000646:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023014,000647:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM
023015,000648:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
023016,000649:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023017,000650:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
023018,000651:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023019,000652:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3
023020,000653:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET

023197,000830:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
023198,000831:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023199,000832:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023200,000833:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023201,000834:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023202,000835: 
023203,000836:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
023204,000837:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
023205,000838:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023206,000839:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023207,000840:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
023208,000841:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
023209,000842:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
023210,000843:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
023211,000844:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
023212,000845:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
023213,000846:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
023214,000847:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
023215,000848:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
023216,000849:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023217,000850:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
023218,000851:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
023219,000852:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
023220,000853:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023221,000854:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023222,000855:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023223,000856:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
023224,000857:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023225,000858:                                                                                                  #    LOSCMFLG      LOKONSW
023226,000859:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
023227,000860:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023228,000861: 24,2756  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT

023402,001035:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
023403,001036:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023404,001037:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023405,001038:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023406,001039:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023407,001040: 
023408,001041:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023409,001042:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023410,001043:                                                                                                  #           TC     R23LEM
023411,001044:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023412,001045:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL        R61LEM
023413,001046:                                                                                                  #    SETMINDB        GOPERF1
023414,001047:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
023415,001048:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
023416,001049:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF PROC  WILL CONTINUE R23
023417,001050:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF TERM  WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
023418,001051:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
023419,001052:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023420,001053:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023421,001054:                                                                                                  #    N.A.
023422,001055:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED-
023423,001056:                                                                                                  #    ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
023424,001057: 24,3220     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
023425,001058: 24,3220                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
023426,001059: 24,3220           05506        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
023427,001060: 24,3221           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
023428,001061: 24,3222           00004                           INHINT                                         
023429,001062: 24,3223           04665                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
023430,001063: 24,3224           40141                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
023431,001064: 24,3225           00003                           RELINT                                         
023432,001065: 24,3226           34727        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
023433,001066: 24,3227           00006                           EXTEND                                         
023434,001067: 24,3230           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                
023435,001068: 24,3231           33270                           CAF      OCT205                                
023436,001069: 24,3232           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
023437,001070: 24,3233           20635                           CADR     GOPERF1                               
023438,001071: 24,3234           03261                           TC       R23LEM2                               #  TERMINATE
023439,001072: 24,3235           03237                           TC       R23LEM11                              #  PROCEDE
023440,001073: 24,3236           03264                           TC       R23LEM3                               #  ENTER- DO ANOTHER MANUVER
023441,001074: 24,3237           00004        R23LEM11           INHINT                                         
023442,001075: 24,3240           04514                           TC       RRLIMCHK                              #  YES - CHECK IF ANTENNA IS WITHIN LIMITS
023443,001076: 24,3241           00035                           ADRES    CDUT                                  
023444,001077: 24,3242           03251                           TC       OUTOFLIM                              #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023445,001078: 24,3243           04665                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  RESTORE DEADBAND TO
023446,001079: 24,3244           40115                           CADR     RESTORDB                              #  ASTRONAUT SELECTED VALUE
023447,001080: 24,3245           00003                           RELINT                                         
023448,001081: 24,3246           05520                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  CLEAR NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
023449,001082: 24,3247           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON

023453,001086: 24,3252           33267                           CAF      OCT501PV

023455,001088: 24,3254           21572                           CADR     PRIOLARM                              #  LIMITS

023472,001105:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
023473,001106:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023474,001107:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023475,001108:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
023476,001109:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023477,001110: 
023478,001111:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
023479,001112:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
023480,001113:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
023481,001114:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
023482,001115:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
023483,001116:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
023484,001117:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
023485,001118:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
023486,001119:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023487,001120:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
023488,001121:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
023489,001122:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
023490,001123:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023491,001124:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
023492,001125:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
023493,001126:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
023494,001127:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023495,001128:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023496,001129:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
023497,001130:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
023498,001131:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023499,001132:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
023500,001133:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023501,001134:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
023502,001135: 24,3271  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
023503,001136: 24,3271                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
023504,001137: 24,3271           05506        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
023505,001138: 24,3272           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
023506,001139: 24,3273           05520                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
023507,001140: 24,3274           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
023508,001141: 24,3275           34746        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
023509,001142: 24,3276           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
023510,001143: 24,3277           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
023511,001144: 24,3300           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
023512,001145: 24,3301           05355        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
023513,001146: 24,3302           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
023514,001147: 24,3303           33336                           CAF      V16N80                                
023515,001148: 24,3304           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
023516,001149: 24,3305           20477                           CADR     PRIODSPR                              
023517,001150: 24,3306           06043                           TC       GOTOV56                               
023518,001151: 24,3307           03313                           TC       R24END                                #  PROCEED EXIT R24 TO P20LEM1
023519,001152: 
023520,001153: 24,3310           03317                           TC       R24LEM3                               #  RECYCLE - CALL R61 TO MANEUVER S/C

023576,001209:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
023577,001210:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

023585,001218:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE.

023598,001231:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS FLAG ARE NOT SET.

023787,001420:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023788,001421: 
023789,001422:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023790,001423:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023791,001424:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023792,001425:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023793,001426:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023794,001427:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023795,001428:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023796,001429:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023797,001430:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023798,001431:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023799,001432:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023800,001433:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023801,001434:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023802,001435:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023803,001436:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023804,001437: 
023805,001438:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023806,001439:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
023807,001440:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
023808,001441: 
023809,001442:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023810,001443:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
023811,001444:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023812,001445:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
023813,001446: 
023814,001447:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
023815,001448: 
023816,001449:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023817,001450: 
023818,001451:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023819,001452: 
023820,001453:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L + 2 (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023821,001454:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023822,001455: 
023823,001456:    4514           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND

023866,001499:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023867,001500: 
023868,001501:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023869,001502:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023870,001503:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023871,001504:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023872,001505:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023873,001506:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023874,001507:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023875,001508:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023876,001509:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023877,001510:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023878,001511:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023879,001512:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023880,001513:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023881,001514:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023882,001515:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023883,001516:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023884,001517:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023885,001518:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023886,001519:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023887,001520:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023888,001521:

023936,001569:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON

A vertical line is drawn next to the log section name and program name. 

023938,001571: 
023939,001572:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023940,001573: 
023941,001574:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
023942,001575:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023943,001576:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023944,001577:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023945,001578:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023946,001579:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023947,001580:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023948,001581:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023949,001582:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023950,001583:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023951,001584:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023952,001585:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023953,001586: 
023954,001587:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
023955,001588:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
023956,001589:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023957,001590: 
023958,001591:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023959,001592:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023960,001593: 
023961,001594:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023962,001595: 
023963,001596:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023964,001597:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023965,001598: 
023966,001599:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023967,001600: 
023968,001601:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023969,001602: 
023970,001603: 24,3337                                           BANK     24                                    
023971,001604: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023972,001605: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023973,001606: 
023974,001607: 25,2053  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023975,001608: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023976,001609: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
023977,001610: 25,2054           05223                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
023978,001611: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.

023985,001618:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023986,001619: 
023987,001620:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023988,001621:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023989,001622:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023990,001623:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023991,001624:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023992,001625:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
023993,001626:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023994,001627:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023995,001628:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023996,001629:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023997,001630:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023998,001631:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023999,001632:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
024000,001633:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
024001,001634:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
024002,001635:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
024003,001636: 
024004,001637:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
024005,001638:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024006,001639:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
024007,001640: 
024008,001641:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
024009,001642: 
024010,001643:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024011,001644:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024012,001645: 
024013,001646:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
024014,001647: 
024015,001648:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
024016,001649: 
024017,001650: 25,2062           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND

024020,001653: 25,2065           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.

024058,001691:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
024059,001692:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024060,001693:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
024061,001694:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
024062,001695:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
024063,001696:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
024064,001697:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
024065,001698:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
024066,001699:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
024067,001700:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
024068,001701:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
024069,001702:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
024070,001703:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
024071,001704:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
024072,001705:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
024073,001706:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
024074,001707:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
024075,001708:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
024076,001709:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
024077,001710:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024078,001711:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
024079,001712:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
024080,001713:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
024081,001714:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
024082,001715: 
024083,001716:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024084,001717:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
024085,001718:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
024086,001719: 
024087,001720:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024088,001721:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
024089,001722: 
024090,001723:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024091,001724:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
024092,001725: 
024093,001726:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024094,001727:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024095,001728: 
024096,001729:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
024097,001730: 
024098,001731:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
024099,001732:

024145,001778:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
024146,001779: 
024147,001780:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
024148,001781:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
024149,001782:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
024150,001783:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
024151,001784:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
024152,001785:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
024153,001786:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
024154,001787:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
024155,001788:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
024156,001789:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
024157,001790:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
024158,001791:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
024159,001792:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
024160,001793:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
024161,001794:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
024162,001795:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
024163,001796:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
024164,001797:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
024165,001798:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
024166,001799:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
024167,001800: 
024168,001801:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024169,001802:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
024170,001803:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
024171,001804:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
024172,001805:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
024173,001806: 
024174,001807:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024175,001808:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
024176,001809: 
024177,001810:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024178,001811:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
024179,001812: 
024180,001813:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024181,001814:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024182,001815: 
024183,001816:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024184,001817:

024237,001870:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
024238,001871: 
024239,001872:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024240,001873:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
024241,001874:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
024242,001875:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
024243,001876:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
024244,001877:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
024245,001878:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
024246,001879:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
024247,001880:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
024248,001881:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
024249,001882:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
024250,001883:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
024251,001884:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
024252,001885:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
024253,001886:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
024254,001887: 
024255,001888:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
024256,001889:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
024257,001890:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
024258,001891:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
024259,001892:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
024260,001893: 
024261,001894:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024262,001895:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
024263,001896: 
024264,001897:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024265,001898:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT

024269,001902:

024271,001904:

024273,001906:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)

024325,001958:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
024326,001959: 
024327,001960:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024328,001961:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
024329,001962:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
024330,001963:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
024331,001964:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
024332,001965:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
024333,001966:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
024334,001967:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
024335,001968:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
024336,001969:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
024337,001970:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
024338,001971:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
024339,001972:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
024340,001973:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024341,001974: 
024342,001975:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024343,001976:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
024344,001977:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
024345,001978: 
024346,001979:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024347,001980:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
024348,001981:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
024349,001982:
